# Issue 32432: Modularization of sagelib: Break out a separate package sagemath-polyhedra

archive/issues_032195.json:
```json
{
    "body": "We define a superset of the distribution **sagemath-categories** (from #29865), called https://pypi.org/project/sagemath-polyhedra/, which is large enough to work with rational polyhedra, including running most doctests\n\nIn:\n- `ZZ`, `QQ`, `RDF`\n- enough of `sage.modules`, `sage.matrix` to do linear algebra over these rings\n- `install_requires` on `pplpy`\n\nOut:\n- real fields other than `RDF`\n- number fields (we conditionalize out doctests that use them - #32652)\n- `sage.symbolic`\n- most of `sage.combinat` (we conditionalize out doctests that use combinatorial examples such as associahedra)\n- `sage.graphs`\n- `sage.plot`\n\nTo test:\n\n```\n$ ./bootstrap && ./sage -sh -c '(cd pkgs/sagemath-polyhedra && SAGE_NUM_THREADS=16 tox -v -v -v)'\n```\nTo run more of the testsuite afterwards:\n\n```\n$ . pkgs/sagemath-polyhedra/.tox/python/bin/activate\n(python) $ (cd $(python -c \"from sage.env import SAGE_SRC; print(SAGE_SRC)\") && sage -tp --environment=sage.all__sagemath_polyhedra sage/geometry)\n...\n(python) $ deactivate\n```\n\nFollow-up steps:\n- redo as distribution with dependency on **sagemath-categories**\n- wheels for this distribution, for **pplpy** and **PyNormaliz**\n- native Windows port\n\n\nCC:  @kliem @tscrim @anneschilling\n\nWork_Issues: git blame -b --first-parent 32432-base.. src/sage/geometry/polyhedron/base.py\n\nAuthor: Matthias Koeppe\n\nBranch: u/mkoeppe/modularization_of_sagelib__break_out_a_separate_package_sagemath_polyhedra\n\nStatus: needs_work\n\nDependencies: #32779, #34195, #33011, #34804, #34855\n\nCommit: 702ee8d5a50971f0022079efeeafb3d522216e65\n\nIssue created by migration from https://trac.sagemath.org/ticket/32432\n\n",

We define a superset of the distribution **sagemath-categories** (from #29865), called https://pypi.org/project/sagemath-polyhedra/, which is large enough to work with rational polyhedra, including running most doctests

In:
- `ZZ`, `QQ`, `RDF`
- enough of `sage.modules`, `sage.matrix` to do linear algebra over these rings
- `install_requires` on `pplpy`

Out:
- real fields other than `RDF`
- number fields (we conditionalize out doctests that use them - #32652)
- `sage.symbolic`
- most of `sage.combinat` (we conditionalize out doctests that use combinatorial examples such as associahedra)
- `sage.graphs`
- `sage.plot`

To test:

```
$ ./bootstrap && ./sage -sh -c '(cd pkgs/sagemath-polyhedra && SAGE_NUM_THREADS=16 tox -v -v -v)'
```
To run more of the testsuite afterwards:

```
$ . pkgs/sagemath-polyhedra/.tox/python/bin/activate
(python) $ (cd $(python -c "from sage.env import SAGE_SRC; print(SAGE_SRC)") && sage -tp --environment=sage.all__sagemath_polyhedra sage/geometry)
...
(python) $ deactivate
```

Follow-up steps:
- redo as distribution with dependency on **sagemath-categories**
- wheels for this distribution, for **pplpy** and **PyNormaliz**
- native Windows port


CC:  @kliem @tscrim @anneschilling

Description changed:
``````diff
--- 
+++ 
@@ -1,3 +1,22 @@
+We define a superset of the distribution **sagemath-categories** (from #29865), called **sagemath-polyhedra** that is large enough to work with rational polyhedra, including running most doctests
+
+In:
+- `ZZ`, `QQ`
+- enough of `sage.modules`, `sage.matrix` to do linear algebra over these rings
+- `install_requires` on `pplpy`
+
+Out:
+- real fields
+- number fields (we conditionalize out doctests that use them - #32652)
+- `sage.symbolic`
+- most of `sage.combinat` (we conditionalize out doctests that use combinatorial examples such as associahedra)
+- `sage.graphs`
+
+To test:
+
+```
+./bootstrap && ./sage -sh -c '(cd pkgs/sagemath-polyhedra && SAGE_NUM_THREADS=16 tox -v -v -v)'
+```
 
 
 Dependencies: #29865, #30022, #32416
``````

{
    "body": "Description changed:\n``````diff\n--- \n+++ \n@@ -1,3 +1,23 @@\n+We define a superset of the distribution **sagemath-categories** (from #29865), called **sagemath-polyhedra** that is large enough to work with rational polyhedra, including running most doctests\n+\n+In:\n+- `ZZ`, `QQ`, `RDF`\n+- enough of `sage.modules`, `sage.matrix` to do linear algebra over these rings\n+- `install_requires` on `pplpy`\n+\n+Out:\n+- real fields other than `RDF`\n+- number fields (we conditionalize out doctests that use them - #32652)\n+- `sage.symbolic`\n+- most of `sage.combinat` (we conditionalize out doctests that use combinatorial examples such as associahedra)\n+- `sage.graphs`\n+- `sage.plot`\n+\n+To test:\n+\n+```\n+./bootstrap && ./sage -sh -c '(cd pkgs/sagemath-polyhedra && SAGE_NUM_THREADS=16 tox -v -v -v)'\n+```\n \n \n Dependencies: #29865, #30022, #32416\n``````\n",

Description changed:
``````diff
--- 
+++ 
@@ -1,3 +1,23 @@
+We define a superset of the distribution **sagemath-categories** (from #29865), called **sagemath-polyhedra** that is large enough to work with rational polyhedra, including running most doctests
+
+In:
+- `ZZ`, `QQ`, `RDF`
+- enough of `sage.modules`, `sage.matrix` to do linear algebra over these rings
+- `install_requires` on `pplpy`
+
+Out:
+- real fields other than `RDF`
+- number fields (we conditionalize out doctests that use them - #32652)
+- `sage.symbolic`
+- most of `sage.combinat` (we conditionalize out doctests that use combinatorial examples such as associahedra)
+- `sage.graphs`
+- `sage.plot`
+
+To test:
+
+```
+./bootstrap && ./sage -sh -c '(cd pkgs/sagemath-polyhedra && SAGE_NUM_THREADS=16 tox -v -v -v)'
+```
 
 
 Dependencies: #29865, #30022, #32416
``````

Description changed:
``````diff
--- 
+++ 
@@ -1,3 +1,28 @@
+We define a superset of the distribution **sagemath-categories** (from #29865), called https://pypi.org/project/sagemath-polyhedra/, which is large enough to work with rational polyhedra, including running most doctests
+
+In:
+- `ZZ`, `QQ`, `RDF`
+- enough of `sage.modules`, `sage.matrix` to do linear algebra over these rings
+- `install_requires` on `pplpy`
+
+Out:
+- real fields other than `RDF`
+- number fields (we conditionalize out doctests that use them - #32652)
+- `sage.symbolic`
+- most of `sage.combinat` (we conditionalize out doctests that use combinatorial examples such as associahedra)
+- `sage.graphs`
+- `sage.plot`
+
+To test:
+
+```
+./bootstrap && ./sage -sh -c '(cd pkgs/sagemath-polyhedra && SAGE_NUM_THREADS=16 tox -v -v -v)'
+```
+
+Follow-up steps:
+- redo as distribution with dependency on **sagemath-categories**
+- wheels for this distribution, for **pplpy** and **PyNormaliz**
+- native Windows port
 
 
 Dependencies: #29865, #30022, #32416
``````

    "body": "Description changed:\n``````diff\n--- \n+++ \n@@ -1,3 +1,36 @@\n+We define a superset of the distribution **sagemath-categories** (from #29865), called https://pypi.org/project/sagemath-polyhedra/, which is large enough to work with rational polyhedra, including running most doctests\n+\n+In:\n+- `ZZ`, `QQ`, `RDF`\n+- enough of `sage.modules`, `sage.matrix` to do linear algebra over these rings\n+- `install_requires` on `pplpy`\n+\n+Out:\n+- real fields other than `RDF`\n+- number fields (we conditionalize out doctests that use them - #32652)\n+- `sage.symbolic`\n+- most of `sage.combinat` (we conditionalize out doctests that use combinatorial examples such as associahedra)\n+- `sage.graphs`\n+- `sage.plot`\n+\n+To test:\n+\n+```\n+$ ./bootstrap && ./sage -sh -c '(cd pkgs/sagemath-polyhedra && SAGE_NUM_THREADS=16 tox -v -v -v)'\n+```\n+To run more of the testsuite afterwards:\n+\n+```\n+$ . pkgs/sagemath-polyhedra/.tox/python/bin/activate\n+(python) $ sage -tp src/sage/geometry/polyhedron\n+...\n+(python) $ deactivate\n+```\n+\n+Follow-up steps:\n+- redo as distribution with dependency on **sagemath-categories**\n+- wheels for this distribution, for **pplpy** and **PyNormaliz**\n+- native Windows port\n \n \n Dependencies: #29865, #30022, #32416\n``````\n",

Description changed:
``````diff
--- 
+++ 
@@ -1,3 +1,36 @@
+We define a superset of the distribution **sagemath-categories** (from #29865), called https://pypi.org/project/sagemath-polyhedra/, which is large enough to work with rational polyhedra, including running most doctests
+
+In:
+- `ZZ`, `QQ`, `RDF`
+- enough of `sage.modules`, `sage.matrix` to do linear algebra over these rings
+- `install_requires` on `pplpy`
+
+Out:
+- real fields other than `RDF`
+- number fields (we conditionalize out doctests that use them - #32652)
+- `sage.symbolic`
+- most of `sage.combinat` (we conditionalize out doctests that use combinatorial examples such as associahedra)
+- `sage.graphs`
+- `sage.plot`
+
+To test:
+
+```
+$ ./bootstrap && ./sage -sh -c '(cd pkgs/sagemath-polyhedra && SAGE_NUM_THREADS=16 tox -v -v -v)'
+```
+To run more of the testsuite afterwards:
+
+```
+$ . pkgs/sagemath-polyhedra/.tox/python/bin/activate
+(python) $ sage -tp src/sage/geometry/polyhedron
+...
+(python) $ deactivate
+```
+
+Follow-up steps:
+- redo as distribution with dependency on **sagemath-categories**
+- wheels for this distribution, for **pplpy** and **PyNormaliz**
+- native Windows port
 
 
 Dependencies: #29865, #30022, #32416
``````

Description changed:
``````diff
--- 
+++ 
@@ -1,3 +1,36 @@
+We define a superset of the distribution **sagemath-categories** (from #29865), called https://pypi.org/project/sagemath-polyhedra/, which is large enough to work with rational polyhedra, including running most doctests
+
+In:
+- `ZZ`, `QQ`, `RDF`
+- enough of `sage.modules`, `sage.matrix` to do linear algebra over these rings
+- `install_requires` on `pplpy`
+
+Out:
+- real fields other than `RDF`
+- number fields (we conditionalize out doctests that use them - #32652)
+- `sage.symbolic`
+- most of `sage.combinat` (we conditionalize out doctests that use combinatorial examples such as associahedra)
+- `sage.graphs`
+- `sage.plot`
+
+To test:
+
+```
+$ ./bootstrap && ./sage -sh -c '(cd pkgs/sagemath-polyhedra && SAGE_NUM_THREADS=16 tox -v -v -v)'
+```
+To run more of the testsuite afterwards:
+
+```
+$ . pkgs/sagemath-polyhedra/.tox/python/bin/activate
+(python) $ sage -tp --environment=sage.all__sagemath_polyhedra src/sage/geometry/polyhedron
+...
+(python) $ deactivate
+```
+
+Follow-up steps:
+- redo as distribution with dependency on **sagemath-categories**
+- wheels for this distribution, for **pplpy** and **PyNormaliz**
+- native Windows port

Description changed:
``````diff
--- 
+++ 
@@ -1,3 +1,36 @@
+We define a superset of the distribution **sagemath-categories** (from #29865), called https://pypi.org/project/sagemath-polyhedra/, which is large enough to work with rational polyhedra, including running most doctests
+
+In:
+- `ZZ`, `QQ`, `RDF`
+- enough of `sage.modules`, `sage.matrix` to do linear algebra over these rings
+- `install_requires` on `pplpy`
+
+Out:
+- real fields other than `RDF`
+- number fields (we conditionalize out doctests that use them - #32652)
+- `sage.symbolic`
+- most of `sage.combinat` (we conditionalize out doctests that use combinatorial examples such as associahedra)
+- `sage.graphs`
+- `sage.plot`
+
+To test:
+
+```
+$ ./bootstrap && ./sage -sh -c '(cd pkgs/sagemath-polyhedra && SAGE_NUM_THREADS=16 tox -v -v -v)'
+```
+To run more of the testsuite afterwards:
+
+```
+$ . pkgs/sagemath-polyhedra/.tox/python/bin/activate
+(python) $ (cd $(python -c "from sage.env import SAGE_SRC; print(SAGE_SRC)") && sage -tp --environment=sage.all__sagemath_polyhedra sage/geometry)
+...
+(python) $ deactivate
+```
+
+Follow-up steps:
+- redo as distribution with dependency on **sagemath-categories**
+- wheels for this distribution, for **pplpy** and **PyNormaliz**
+- native Windows port
 
 
 Dependencies: #29865, #30022, #32416
``````
